< review>
I was just at this place. I've been wanting to try it out since they opened and my mom and I walked by and saw that Stacks of firewood outside. Us being from Latin countries, we knew that when a place has stacks of firewood outside, tl;dr, "There's the good sh!t"

So I ordered a slice.

It was 'Amazing'.

If you need any other adjective to describe a pizza, please move along.

The crust was perfect, the small spheres of pepperoni delight were resplendent and exquisite. And the cheese. OMG, the cheese, not only did it savor like genuine alchemical dairy, it oozed off the edges on particular parts of the slice to give that genuine pizza experience.

This only makes me wonder; they put so much quality into a 'single' slice, I wonder what else their menu tastes like.<//review>

< Review>
Came here for date night since we live a couple of blocks away and one of the servers is an acquaintance of my BF, so we decided to check it out. The decor is clean and very homey, having been in Italy just a few weeks prior, the ambiance definitely reminded me of my trip. They have a great wine selection and with the two of us being new to the wine game, the Somme gave us a great recommendation based on our preferences.

Everything on that menu looked so good; but we settled on the Antico steak and the cappelini al limone, and we weren‚Äôt disappointed. The pasta was cooked perfectly, and the two pieces of anchovy on top complemented the citrus flavor of the sauce very well. The steak was tender and very well seasoned on its own, but the accompanying salsa verde took it to another level.

DO NOT SKIP OUT ON THE HONEYCOMB ICE CREAM!! One of the best ice creams I‚Äôve had. They add a little bit of salt and olive oil, and somehow that makes it even better.

The staff were all great and very accommodating. I really appreciated that they didn‚Äôt come up during every course and asked if everything was ok while I was busy stuffing my face with tasty food. I think the clean and empty plates coming back to the kitchen spoke for us.<//Review>

<text>Stopped in for a minor life celebration with my partner, we grabbed the final reservation for the evening at 9:30pm.

Immediately, we were hit with the beautiful decor and excellent service. Ambience was on point as we were seated, though it became immediately obvious that my partner and I would not be having an intimate evening as we could barely hear anything we said to one another. Atmosphere was cozy with long tables for larger parties and tables off to the sides for parties of 2-4. It was very nice to be able to look into the kitchen and see our chefs hard at work.

The wine list is extensive and we shared 2 glasses of champagne which was delightful and complimented our meal well. Someone with more of a sommelier‚Äôs

We decided to split the ‚ÄúBurrata‚Äù as our opener which was a delightful breakdown of a typical caprese salad. We followed up with the ‚ÄúZiti‚Äù for myself and the ‚ÄúMaccheroni‚Äù for my partner, along with some bread. Both dishes were excellent, unique flavor pairings and depth you rarely find outside of a white tablecloth type restaurant. We both found ourselves unimpressed with the pasta, however. It is not bad, but didn‚Äôt taste as fresh as, say, Pasta Sisters. The bread was excellent, crunchy on the outside but soft on the inside and perfectly salted. Finally, we did get some ice cream which was, by far, our favorite part of the meal. Fresh and ultra creamy, it was beyond exquisite.

At the end of the night I still had leftovers and our server got me some more bread to have with my pasta which was such a nice touch. Overall, we both had a wonderful evening with excellent service but for the price, the pasta was only good, not great, and we can find great pasta in so many places. Happy this place exists and I hope we may come back once it‚Äôs found surer footing!< /text><Pictures>None</Pictures>< Response>

<user_id>101762313220855699516< /user_id><name>Sarah Godlove< /name><Date>1604304858759</Date><rate>4< /rate><Text>We stopped by for the first time on a recent Wednesday to enjoy a bottle of wine by the pond. Vitagliano is primarily a wedding/event venue and their grounds are absolutely beautiful. We were in the mood for a dry white and were offered a taste of their cabernet ros√© and Moscato. I don‚Äôt like sweet wines and was pleasantly surprised that the Moscato was quite good ‚Äì crisp, dry and very fruity. It was hard to choose, but we opted for a bottle of the ros√©. I appreciated that they automatically gave us an ice bucket to keep it chilled. I had read that you can preorder charcuterie, sandwiches, salads, desserts. We didn‚Äôt order ahead, but I asked and they happened to have a few small charcuterie plates available. Their food is provided locally through E.A.T. Marketplace. The charcuterie was very small for the price and the few strawberries in it were mushy and a bit moldy underneath! We brought it to their attention and were offered another one, which wasn‚Äôt much better. I think the charcuterie containers had been around for a day or two, so perhaps if we had preordered, the food would have been better/fresher. So the food was a bit of a disappointment and I‚Äôm not wild about having to preorder 24 hours in advance since we tend to stop in to wineries as the mood strikes us. But on the upside, the ros√© was refreshing and we enjoyed sitting by the pond and wandering the grounds a bit. We‚Äôd definitely return ‚Äì the grounds are truly magical and this is the perfect setting for relaxing with a good bottle of wine.</Text>< pictures>

<review>The food here is relatively good, especially the Salt And Pepper fish filet. The portions are fairly large with prices that are reasonable.
The restaurant itself does need to be updated, as it appears to be a little worse for wear.  The booth seats are lumpy and worn. The bathrooms are filthy, so hopefully you don't need to use them.
Parking is limited, so it's sometimes better to come a little sooner than peak eating times. On Sundays and after 6 pm on other days, you can park in the lot belonging to the tire store adjacent to the restaurant. This alleviates the parking problem a great deal.
Overall, this is a good place for Chinese food, but don't expect fine dining.< /review><time>1509567128050</time><Response>None</Response>< rating>
